</style><div class="fluid-engine fe-633c441ffaf0dd20a38c2f08"><div class="fe-block fe-block-94d5890fb61d45f17c8b"><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-94d5890fb61d45f17c8b"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h1 style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Space Pirate Trainer<br>2016</h1>
</div>



</div></div></div><div class="fe-block fe-block-ca9e40e31ef41393d36f"><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-ca9e40e31ef41393d36f"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="sqsrte-large" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Space Pirate Trainer puts you inside one of those awesome classic 80s arcade cabinets, where you’ll fight off relentless waves of droids with all the weapons and gadgets a Space Pirate would ever need. Pick up your blasters, tie up your sneakers, and dance your way into the Space Pirate Trainer hall of fame!</p><p class="sqsrte-large" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Launched in 2016 as one of the first titles specifically built for room-scale VR, the game has far exceeded our expectations in terms of user feedback, media attention, and sold units. It is considered <strong>the most seminal wave-based shooter in the history of modern VR</strong>.</p><p class="sqsrte-large" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">SPT was an official launch title on Steam VR (HTC Vive), Oculus Touch, Microsoft Mixed Reality, and Oculus (Meta) Quest, and was ported to PlayStation VR in 2018.</p>
</div>



</div></div></div><div class="fe-block fe-block-yui_3_17_2_1_1665576346314_11736"><div class="sqs-block code-block sqs-block-code" data-block-type="23" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1665576346314_11736"><div class="sqs-block-content"><h4><span class="highlight">In 2021 the <a href="/games/spacepiratetrainerdx"><u>DX edition</u></a> added two kick-ass multiplayer modes: VERSUS and, more importantly, ARENA.</span></h4></div></div></div></div></div>
    </div>
  
  </div>
  
</section>
